  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_71dc0a82-b740-444b-9ea2-bcc1ae4fa73e'

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9860297679397479747"><b>***3.75 stars***</b><br/><br/>This was such a cute read!! A Different Kind of Fairy Tale was the story of Alex and Stella, who have been neighbors and best friends for years. Basically, what happens is that the two fake a relationship when Stella is hired by her ex-boyfriend and the women he cheated on her with to take their wedding photos. And then that fake relationship becomes real, and so much more...<br/><br/>Overall I really do like the book, but something that confused me was that under genre it’s described as e</span>
  <span id="freeText9860297679397479747" style="display:none"><b>***3.75 stars***</b><br /><br />This was such a cute read!! A Different Kind of Fairy Tale was the story of Alex and Stella, who have been neighbors and best friends for years. Basically, what happens is that the two fake a relationship when Stella is hired by her ex-boyfriend and the women he cheated on her with to take their wedding photos. And then that fake relationship becomes real, and so much more...<br /><br />Overall I really do like the book, but something that confused me was that under genre it’s described as erotic when it’s really not. If I remember right, there’s only one, maybe two sex scenes. Anyway, if your looking to pass some time, pick this up!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer437036126320010080"><strong>3 Not-a-Fairy-Tale Stars</strong><br/><br/>Stella, (love that name) has always been one of the guys. She doesn't do makeup, fancy clothing and is finally successful. The only problem, she sucks at relationships. Her last boyfriend cheated on her with her best friend. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423848ra/844670.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And now, she lives next to the best looking guy she's ever known, Alex.   <span id="freeText437036126320010080" style="display:none"><strong>3 Not-a-Fairy-Tale Stars</strong><br><br>Stella, (love that name) has always been one of the guys. She doesn't do makeup, fancy clothing and is finally successful. The only problem, she sucks at relationships. Her last boyfriend cheated on her with her best friend. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423848ra/844670.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now, she lives next to the best looking guy she's ever known, Alex. She's also best friends with him.<br><br>Alex, has always been tempted by Stella. But to prevent losing a friend, he decides to not act on his feelings. Until one day, her asshole ex-boyfriend requests to have her photograph his wedding with the girl he cheated on her with. What.A.Dick.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423848ra/844671.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because Stella has self-esteem issues, she decides to tell her ex that she's dating Alex. <br><br><strong>Why I couldn't rate this book higher:</strong><br><br>-Stella starts out as a really strong character, she turns into a whiny mess. Completely falls apart when she finds a pair of ladies underwear while at Alex's house. I can't stand reading characters who don't know their self-worth and have to have every other character tell them how awesome they are.<br><br>- I personally don't like relationships which start before the book actually begins. I like read the entire development instead of flashbacks.<br><br><strong>What I liked:</strong><br><br>- Sexy times were hot.<br>- It was sweet, and I truly felt that these two characters were good for each other.<br>- It was free :)<br><br><br>Overall, nothing groundbreaking. But it was fun, angsty, and made me smile. </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer526986615" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15525276738035442232">4/4.5*<br/><br/>Ohhhhh, this was a gem!<br/><br/>I really liked the writing in this book, I was totally drawn in to the story from the first page. This is a contemporary love story, with all the elements I like ... angst, love, romance, suspense...<br/><br/>Alex and Stella were friends for 3 years before this story begins...I liked this premise because it makes it feel very realistic. Also I enjoyed Stella, she wasn't your typical model beautiful girly girl, quite the opposite! <br/><br/>The overall plot is predictable .. in that wond</span>
  <span id="freeText15525276738035442232" style="display:none">4/4.5*<br /><br />Ohhhhh, this was a gem!<br /><br />I really liked the writing in this book, I was totally drawn in to the story from the first page. This is a contemporary love story, with all the elements I like ... angst, love, romance, suspense...<br /><br />Alex and Stella were friends for 3 years before this story begins...I liked this premise because it makes it feel very realistic. Also I enjoyed Stella, she wasn't your typical model beautiful girly girl, quite the opposite! <br /><br />The overall plot is predictable .. in that wonderful "butterflies in tummy" way! You just know it's going to be ok but watching it unfold is very emotional. I cried more than once during this book, that's how deeply it drew me in. I really felt the emotions being felt by these characters. Also the supporting characters were not lacking in depth, they were a great addition to the story.<br /><br />This is very similar in style to the Neighbour from Hell series and if you liked those you WILL like this. It is very funny in parts, sexy in others, gushingly romantic at times and overall a fairy tale story..very well executed x<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText8877517944307133537" style="display:none">Let me get something clear: This is not a five-star book. <br /><br />I need to get this out of the way, first. <br /><br /><u>What this book is to me</u><br />I have read this book numerous times, before goodreads and after. <br /><b>A Different Kind of Fairy Tale</b> is a....comfort book, I suppose. I read it over &amp; over &amp; over, loving it every. Single. Time. Therefore, I'm a bit biased in this review. <br /><br /><u>A bit about our girl, Stella.</u> <br />This girl, is a total nut. She is a serious tomboy, has no idea what to do with eye shadow, eyeliner (or which is which). She never wears a stitch of make up, and a pair of jeans, a t-shirt and a ponytail is her everyday, thing. She's also got a wide and colorful vocabulary. <br /><br /><i>"If you drop another pass, I swear I'm going to jump through this TV and rip your balls off!"</i><br /><br />...especially when it comes to football, or more specifically the Green Bay Predators. <br /><br /><i>Stella: "This is serious business. They are in the playoffs; but if they don't get their heads out of their asses, its going to be a short run. I'm simply motivating them; and if small innocent objects get broken in the meantime, so be it. And if Kyle is scared of little old me, his crew at the firehouse should be concerned about him watching their backs." </i> <br /><br />Stella is actually a bit insecure. Her mother growing up (forgive me, not mother "egg donor") was always comparing her to her sister, Victoria, and telling to lose a few pounds, cake on makeup and find tighter clothes. Then they wouldn't see how ugly she really was. In between asking Stella for money, of course. <br /><br />Due to Stella's mom, Stella and Victoria learned the importance of hard work. Both girls own their own businesses, and Stella's is a photography studio, where she spends most of her time. <br /><br />Along with that, Stella's boyfriend three years ago; Kevin, she found was cheating on her with her best friend, Heidi. <br /><br /><i>Heidi: "It's not what you think!" <br />Stella: "You weren't just riding boyfriend like a whore on a rollercoaster. I really should get to the eye doctor, then, because that's exactly what I saw. Now, unless you want to lose the use of your right hand, I suggest you let go of my arm." </i> <br /><br /><u>Alex</u> <br />He lives next door Stella, his 2A to Stella's 2B. He works for himself, building software websites. He is actually a millionaire, or as Victoria says; <i>has more money than God,</i> but you could never tell, looking at him. He wears jeans drives a (Toyota, I think?), and lives in an apartment and the only thing that shows his wealth is his "toys" (electronics). <br /><br />He has also always loved Stella, almost as much as he loves her food. <br /><br /><u>Alex and Stella.</u><br />They are neighbors, they have each others house keys but almost never lock their doors so the other can just come in. <br /><br /><i>Kyle: "Friends that can't keep their eyes off each other maybe; the last time we went to the bar you practically took a piss on her leg to mark your territory when any guy asked her to dance." <br /><br />Alex: "She could do better than those guys. I was just saving her from wasting her time on losers." Really, it was the least he could do as her friend.<br /><br />Kyle: "What about a few months ago when you had a date with Tina or Gina or whatever the hell her name was; Stella jus happened to need your help on a simple plumbing problem, which we both know she could have done herself. Actually, every time you have a date she walks into your apartment with some question or problem. Anytime we all hang out together, it's like the two of you are an old married couple. You eat off each others plates, snuggle on the couch during movies, and spend all your free time together." </i> <br /><br />Stella and Alex are basically roommates...with two apartments. Eat at her house, hang out at both, go to their separate rooms to sleep at night. It's cute, except their both pining after the other, secretly, scared to lose their friendship. <br /><br />What actually brought them together was food. <br /><br /><i>Alex: "So you like to cook? Are you any good or are these cookbooks your attempt not to poison people?" </i><br /><br /><u>The Romance</u> <br />The Romance was really cute! <br />I'm not giving anything away. <br /><br /><u>The Plot</u> <br />1. "The Romance" There's the transition from besties to lovers <br />2. "Tweedle dee &amp; Tweedle dumb" <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Stella's cheating bastard ex returns. Kevin? Remember him and Heidi from above? They want Stella to photograph their wedding, on Valentines Day, and Stella, being the bigger person and wanting to show them that they didn't break her, agrees.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br />3. "Skull and Crossbones" <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Stella's mom dies.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />4. "Heidi is a whore in Whoreland" <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He thinks Stella is cheating on her, and is wrong. <br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br /><u>Characters</u> <br /><b>Lindsey</b> <br />She is a little firecracker, albeit short one. <br /><i>Are you sure?   <span id="freeText13222618451632748227" style="display:none">Stella &amp; Alex are best friends from the minute they meet on move in day. Words you might her come out of a sailors mouth started flying in the hallway as Alex was trying to figure out a way how to cut loose his current girlfriend who was sitting in his livingroom.           <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17347619-a-different-kind-of-fairy-tale">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1198204385" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7244401933903211007"><strong>Well rounded story</strong><br/><br/>A romance budding between two best friends; Stella and Alex. Stella comes from a less than desirable childhood and upbringing, with Alex having had a picture perfect life. We follow through these two coming to their senses with their feelings for each other, and having to work through the tested waters of every new relationship. <br/><br/>While this wasn't my favourite romance story, it holds a number of good qualities. The writing is well done, with good description. Character developme</span>
  <span id="freeText7244401933903211007" style="display:none"><strong>Well rounded story</strong><br /><br />A romance budding between two best friends; Stella and Alex. Stella comes from a less than desirable childhood and upbringing, with Alex having had a picture perfect life. We follow through these two coming to their senses with their feelings for each other, and having to work through the tested waters of every new relationship. <br /><br />While this wasn't my favourite romance story, it holds a number of good qualities. The writing is well done, with good description. Character development was great, giving enough detail to feel with and for them. I just had a hard time connecting to the story line and felt like I was pushing myself to finish. I am interested in seeing how life plays out for the supporting characters, though. A solid story, I will recommend to fellow contemporary romance readers. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7244401933903211007" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Gabrielle Puri" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16480679-gabrielle-puri"><img alt="Gabrielle Puri" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420294363p2/16480679.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

<div id="review_2284187515" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2284187515" />
    <a title="Stacy Sabala" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21732632-stacy-sabala"><img alt="Stacy Sabala" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425568751p2/21732632.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2284187515?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacy Sabala" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacy Sabala" href="/user/show/21732632-stacy-sabala">Stacy Sabala</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17347619-a-different-kind-of-fairy-tale">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21732632-stacy-sabala?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2284187515" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5754307762975730926">Book Review- A Different Kind of Fairy Tale by Morgan Rayne<br/><br/>Stella Howe lives by herself and owns her own photography business. Her best friend, Alex, lives next door. They met three years ago when she moved in. They remain best friends. Stella has noticed how gorgeous Alex is but she is afraid to ruin the friendship. She takes a leap of faith when her ex wants her to be his wedding photographer. With her sister’s help she shows Alex how she feels. He has felt the same way and things are even bet</span>
  <span id="freeText5754307762975730926" style="display:none">Book Review- A Different Kind of Fairy Tale by Morgan Rayne<br /><br />Stella Howe lives by herself and owns her own photography business. Her best friend, Alex, lives next door. They met three years ago when she moved in. They remain best friends. Stella has noticed how gorgeous Alex is but she is afraid to ruin the friendship. She takes a leap of faith when her ex wants her to be his wedding photographer. With her sister’s help she shows Alex how she feels. He has felt the same way and things are even better between them.<br />Unfortunately, an enemy from the past refuses to let Stella end up better than she did. Sabotage is in the works as Stella and Alex become the targets.<br />I like how Stella was a complete tomboy. She loved watching football and refused to be a clique’. Unfortunately, her self-esteem with men was low, thanks to her mother and ex. Her fear to open up is pretty obvious and I love how the object of her affections is Alex. He comes across as sigh-worthy and completely genuine. He is exactly what she needs. <br />I’m shocked at how devious the ex-friend is. I was waiting for Stella to take her out. I missed that satisfaction. That was one thing that didn’t happen, a true confrontation between the two. Stella’s sister, Victoria, was an awesome character. She was almost scary with her dynamo personality and protective nature. Loved her.<br />Then ending was fabulous and I can’t wait to see what happens next. Great read. I give it a 4 out of 5.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5754307762975730926" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('iiySbPXNTSA16JPso4KPyis5lplrS1iYNKqfG0TKC0Rl3huQVivxGEBoPW903GYGTgkmwuqdAtvM8uTgPW2m9g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XFmQ+6H7QPcSj/9dan6HmrI7USmF0gLM7DzddlaqmkWzqxkHAh38z2cPUd69IG5W1wvhcgQEWI8UZKaNLw039w==')})
  }

This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
